DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Set non-interactive for apt
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  # Install system dependencies
  RUN apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          g++ \
          gcc \
          cmake \
          git \
          python3.9 \
          python3.9-venv \
          python3-pip \
          pkg-config \
          make \
          valgrind \
          lcov \
          cppcheck \
          gdb \
          wget \
          unzip \
          zeal \
          ca-certificates \
          libssl-dev \
          locales \
          libffi-dev && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.9 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set locale (for Zeal/docset tools if needed)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Create project directory
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  # Install mkcert (latest release as of writing)
  RUN wget -O /tmp/mkcert https://github.com/FiloSottile/mkcert/releases/download/v1.4.4/mkcert-v1.4.4-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x /tmp/mkcert && \
      mv /tmp/mkcert /usr/local/bin/mkcert && \
      mkcert -install
  # Optional: Install vcpkg and conan (package managers)
  RUN git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/microsoft/vcpkg.git /opt/vcpkg && \
      /opt/vcpkg/bootstrap-vcpkg.sh && \
      python3 -m pip install conan
  ENV PATH="/opt/vcpkg:${PATH}"
  # Install doctest (testing framework) via vcpkg for local use
  RUN /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install doctest
  # Install nlohmann-json via vcpkg (optional), or user may supply their own / include via CMake
  RUN /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install nlohmann-json
  # (Optional) Install Meson and Spack if needed for alternative build systems
  RUN python3 -m pip install meson && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/spack/spack.git /opt/spack
  # (Optional) Install mkdocs and requirements for documentation generation
  RUN python3 -m pip install mkdocs mkdocs-material
  # (Optional) Install PyYAML and watchdog for serve_header.py
  RUN python3 -m pip install PyYAML watchdog
  # Set up GDB pretty printer (user should add their own script as needed)
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.gdbinit.d
  # By default, don't copy project files (assume user will mount at /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json)
  # Uncomment below lines if building with a Docker context containing the codebase:
  # COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  # Set default working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  # Set entrypoint to bash for interactive use
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

           chmod +x mkcert-v1.4.4-linux-amd64 && sudo mv mkcert-v1.4.4-linux-amd64 /usr/local/bin/mkcert
           mkcert -install
           mkcert localhost
           mv localhost.pem localhost-key.pem /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json/

      chmod +x /tmp/mkcert && \
      mv /tmp/mkcert /usr/local/bin/mkcert && \
      mkcert -install
  # Optional: Install vcpkg and conan (package managers)
  RUN git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/microsoft/vcpkg.git /opt/vcpkg && \
      /opt/vcpkg/bootstrap-vcpkg.sh && \
      python3 -m pip install conan
  ENV PATH="/opt/vcpkg:${PATH}"
  # Install doctest (testing framework) via vcpkg for local use
  RUN /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install doctest
  # Install nlohmann-json via vcpkg (optional), or user may supply their own / include via CMake
  RUN /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install nlohmann-json
  # (Optional) Install Meson and Spack if needed for alternative build systems
  RUN python3 -m pip install meson && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/spack/spack.git /opt/spack
  # (Optional) Install mkdocs and requirements for documentation generation
  RUN python3 -m pip install mkdocs mkdocs-material
  # (Optional) Install PyYAML and watchdog for serve_header.py
  RUN python3 -m pip install PyYAML watchdog
  # Set up GDB pretty printer (user should add their own script as needed)
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.gdbinit.d
  # By default, don't copy project files (assume user will mount at /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json)
  # Uncomment below lines if building with a Docker context containing the codebase:
  # COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  # Set default working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  # Set entrypoint to bash for interactive use
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  # Set non-interactive for apt
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  # Add set -ex for better error logging and install system dependencies
  RUN set -ex && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          g++ \
          gcc \
          cmake \
          git \
          python3.10 \
          python3.10-venv \
          python3-pip \
          pkg-config \
          make \
          valgrind \
          lcov \
          cppcheck \
          gdb \
          wget \
          unzip \
          zeal \
          ca-certificates \
          libssl-dev \
          locales \
          libffi-dev && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.10 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Set locale (for Zeal/docset tools if needed)
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  # Create project directory
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  # Install mkcert (latest release as of writing)
  RUN set -ex && \
      wget -O /tmp/mkcert https://github.com/FiloSottile/mkcert/releases/download/v1.4.4/mkcert-v1.4.4-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x /tmp/mkcert && \
      mv /tmp/mkcert /usr/local/bin/mkcert && \
      mkcert -install
  # Install vcpkg (clone and bootstrap) and conan, with better diagnostics
  RUN set -ex && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/microsoft/vcpkg.git /opt/vcpkg && \
      /opt/vcpkg/bootstrap-vcpkg.sh
  RUN python3 -m pip install conan
  ENV PATH="/opt/vcpkg:${PATH}"
  # Install doctest (testing framework) via vcpkg for local use
  RUN set -ex && /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install doctest
  # Install nlohmann-json via vcpkg (optional), or user may supply their own / include via CMake
  RUN set -ex && /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install nlohmann-json
  # (Optional) Install Meson and Spack if needed for alternative build systems
  RUN python3 -m pip install meson && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/spack/spack.git /opt/spack
  # (Optional) Install mkdocs and requirements for documentation generation
  RUN python3 -m pip install mkdocs mkdocs-material
  # (Optional) Install PyYAML and watchdog for serve_header.py
  RUN python3 -m pip install PyYAML watchdog
  # Set up GDB pretty printer (user should add their own script as needed)
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.gdbinit.d
  # By default, don't copy project files (assume user will mount at /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json)
  # Uncomment below lines if building with a Docker context containing the codebase:
  # COPY . /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  # Set default working directory
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  # Set entrypoint to bash for interactive use
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN set -ex && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          g++ \
          gcc \
          cmake \
          git \
          python3.10 \
          python3.10-venv \
          python3-pip \
          pkg-config \
          make \
          valgrind \
          lcov \
          cppcheck \
          gdb \
          wget \
          unzip \
          zeal \
          ca-certificates \
          libssl-dev \
          locales \
          libffi-dev && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.10 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  RUN set -ex && \
      wget -O /tmp/mkcert https://github.com/FiloSottile/mkcert/releases/download/v1.4.4/mkcert-v1.4.4-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x /tmp/mkcert && \
      mv /tmp/mkcert /usr/local/bin/mkcert && \
      mkcert -install
  # Install vcpkg (clone and bootstrap) and conan, with additional diagnostics
  RUN set -ex && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/microsoft/vcpkg.git /opt/vcpkg && \
      cd /opt/vcpkg && \
      ./bootstrap-vcpkg.sh || (cat /opt/vcpkg/bootstrap*.log || true; exit 1)
  RUN python3 -m pip install conan
  ENV PATH="/opt/vcpkg:${PATH}"
  RUN set -ex && /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install doctest
  RUN set -ex && /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install nlohmann-json
  RUN python3 -m pip install meson && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/spack/spack.git /opt/spack
  RUN python3 -m pip install mkdocs mkdocs-material
  RUN python3 -m pip install PyYAML watchdog
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.gdbinit.d
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

          git \

      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8

  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  RUN set -ex && \
      wget -O /tmp/mkcert https://github.com/FiloSottile/mkcert/releases/download/v1.4.4/mkcert-v1.4.4-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x /tmp/mkcert && \
      mv /tmp/mkcert /usr/local/bin/mkcert && \
      mkcert -install
  # Install vcpkg (clone and bootstrap) and conan, with additional diagnostics
  RUN set -ex && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/microsoft/vcpkg.git /opt/vcpkg && \

      ./opt/vcpkg/bootstrap-vcpkg.sh || (ls -l /opt/vcpkg/; cat /opt/vcpkg/bootstrap*.log || true; exit 1)
  RUN python3 -m pip install conan
  ENV PATH="/opt/vcpkg:${PATH}"
  RUN set -ex && /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install doctest
  RUN set -ex && /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install nlohmann-json
  RUN python3 -m pip install meson && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/spack/spack.git /opt/spack
  RUN python3 -m pip install mkdocs mkdocs-material
  RUN python3 -m pip install PyYAML watchdog
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.gdbinit.d
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04
  ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  RUN set -ex && \
      apt-get update && \
      apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
          build-essential \
          g++ \
          gcc \
          cmake \
          git \
          python3.10 \
          python3.10-venv \
          python3-pip \
          pkg-config \
          make \
          valgrind \
          lcov \
          cppcheck \
          gdb \
          wget \
          unzip \
          zeal \
          ca-certificates \
          libssl-dev \
          locales \
          libffi-dev \
          curl \
          zip && \
      ln -sf /usr/bin/python3.10 /usr/local/bin/python3 && \
      python3 -m pip install --upgrade pip && \
      rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  RUN locale-gen en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANG=en_US.UTF-8
  ENV LANGUAGE=en_US:en
  ENV LC_ALL=en_US.UTF-8
  RUN mkdir -p /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  RUN set -ex && \
      wget -O /tmp/mkcert https://github.com/FiloSottile/mkcert/releases/download/v1.4.4/mkcert-v1.4.4-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x /tmp/mkcert && \
      mv /tmp/mkcert /usr/local/bin/mkcert && \
      mkcert -install
  # Install vcpkg (clone and bootstrap) and conan, with additional diagnostics
  RUN set -ex && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/microsoft/vcpkg.git /opt/vcpkg && \
      ls -l /opt/vcpkg/ && \
      test -x /opt/vcpkg/bootstrap-vcpkg.sh && \
      /opt/vcpkg/bootstrap-vcpkg.sh || (ls -l /opt/vcpkg/; cat /opt/vcpkg/bootstrap*.log || true; exit 1)
  RUN python3 -m pip install conan
  ENV PATH="/opt/vcpkg:${PATH}"
  RUN set -ex && /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install doctest
  RUN set -ex && /opt/vcpkg/vcpkg install nlohmann-json
  RUN python3 -m pip install meson && \
      git clone --depth 1 https://github.com/spack/spack.git /opt/spack
  RUN python3 -m pip install mkdocs mkdocs-material
  RUN python3 -m pip install PyYAML watchdog
  RUN mkdir -p /root/.gdbinit.d
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data/nlohmann_json
  ENTRYPOINT ["/bin/bash"]
